          (478)\
          EXT. PARK - DAY\
          \
\pard\intbl\itap2\pardeftab720\sl320\partightenfactor0

\f3\b0 \cf2           For a few seconds we watch A MAN (20s) and a WOMAN (20s) on a\

          a word.\
\pard\intbl\itap2\pardeftab720\sl320\partightenfactor0

\f2\b \cf2           \
          \
\pard\intbl\itap2\pardeftab720\sl320\partightenfactor0

\f3\b0 \cf2           CLOSE ON her HAND, covering his. Notice the wedding ring. No\
          words are spoken. Tom looks at her the way every woman wants\
          to be looked at.\
\pard\intbl\itap2\pardeftab720\sl320\partightenfactor0

\f2\b \cf2           \
\pard\intbl\itap2\pardeftab720\sl320\partightenfactor0

\f3\b0 \cf2           A DISTINGUISHED VOICE begins to speak to us.\

\f2\b \cf2           \

\pard\intbl\itap2\pardeftab720\sl320\partightenfactor0

\f3\b0 \cf2                     This is a story of boy meets girl.\

          \

          (1)\
          INT CONFERENCE ROOM - DAY\
          \
\pard\intbl\itap2\pardeftab720\sl320\partightenfactor0

\f3\b0 \cf2           The boy is TOM HANSEN. He sits at a very long rectangular\
          conference table. The walls are lined with framed blow-up\
          sized greeting cards. Tom, dark hair and blue eyes, wears a t-\
          shirt under his sports coat and Adidas tennis shoes to\
          balance out the corporate dress code. He looks pretty bored.\
\pard\intbl\itap2\pardeftab720\sl320\partightenfactor0

\f2\b \cf2           \
                              NARRATOR\
\pard\intbl\itap2\pardeftab720\sl320\partightenfactor0

\f3\b0 \cf2                     The boy, Tom Hansen of Margate, New\
                    Jersey, grew up believing that he'd\
                    never truly be happy until the day\
                    he met his... "soulmate."\
\pard\intbl\itap2\pardeftab720\sl320\partightenfactor0
